The United States Fears That Japanese People Will Destroy American Fortresses 100

Military Administration Case in Honolulu

Already Submitted to the House of Representatives for Discussion

Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun says: The military administration case for the Hawaiian Islands proposed by US Navy Committee Chairman Britten has already been submitted to the House of Representatives' Review Committee for discussion. Britten explained the reasons for the case, saying that if the residences of Japanese people living in Honolulu were searched, a Japanese conspiracy to destroy American fortresses would be discovered. He also said that the natives of Honolulu and the Japanese people cannot be regarded as honest American citizens. Washington State elected Republican Congressman Albert Johnson also echoed Britten's statement. As a result, the atmosphere of the committee suddenly became tense. The most noteworthy thing is that the famous wartime reporter of the United States, Gobons, also strongly advocated the necessity of implementing the military administration case in Honolulu.

Red Bandits Withdraw from Zhangzhou 101

Fleeing to Nanjing and Longyan

Fuzhou Correspondence: Fang Shengtao, Acting Chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, recently went to Tong'an with Commissioner Lin Zhiyuan to supervise the army in counterattacking Zhangzhou. Upon hearing the news, the Zhangzhou Red Bandits immediately changed their strategy. On May 26, they abandoned Shima and retreated the front-line bandits into Zhangzhou. On the 27th, they abandoned Zhangzhou again and retreated to Nanjing. Chen Guohui's troops of the First Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army stationed in Tong'an sent a battalion of soldiers on the 28th to inspect the vicinity of Shima and Zhangcheng from Jiaowei. Seeing that there were indeed no traces of bandits, but fearing that there were still tricks, they returned. On the morning of the 29th, Wu Shu's replenishment battalion of the Forty-ninth Division (compiled from local bandits in Zhangzhou) was the first to enter Zhangcheng. In the afternoon, Fang Shengtao ordered the two brigade commanders, Chen Guohui and Yang Fengnian, to lead a team each to continue to enter Zhangma from Tong'an Haicheng. Local order gradually became safe. Fang Shengtao himself decided to lead Lin Shuguo's Marine Corps into Zhang on the 30th to command the troops to pursue Nanjing. Yesterday (30th), he reported the recovery of Zhangma to the Provincial Government and the Central Government, stating that the bandit suppression military affairs are currently progressing, and he must stay in Zhang to command the front-line troops, making it difficult to return to the province temporarily. The rear defense is still entrusted to Liu Heding. Liu's division has three infantry regiments and a special service battalion in the province, stationed at the northeast gates. Liu also plans to convene a joint meeting of the party, government, and military in the coming days to discuss comprehensive security measures.

Another report: The Red Bandits withdrew from Zhangzhou on the 26th and moved to Jinlong Mountain and other places. Chen Peiyu's battalion of the Provincial Defense First Brigade first entered Zhangcheng on the 28th. Later, due to the disorder in the county and to prevent the Red Bandits from having tricks, they withdrew from the city again that night. On the morning of the 29th, Fang Shengtao, upon hearing the report, sent Wang Zuqing's Second Regiment to assist in Jinjiang to maintain defense and sent a team to pursue and suppress them. Fang also sent Cai Zhuchan to the county government to maintain county administration. Jiangdong Bridge and the second and third districts were also divided into fleeing Nanjing and Longyan by the masses and alliances after. The bandits in Shima also retreated to Nanjing. Lin Shuguo then led Huang Maohe's troops to advance to Shima on the 30th (May 31st).

Peng Dehuai Suffers a Miserable Defeat on the Border of Jiangxi and Hunan 102

More Than 2,000 Bandits Killed or Wounded in the Battle of Rucheng

Nanchang Correspondence: The pseudo-3rd Army Group of the communist bandits, led by Peng Dehuai, with more than 10,000 troops and 3,000 to 4,000 guns, has been using the treacherous terrain of the border area to contain the troops of Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Hunan provinces since they fled to the border area of Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Hunan, allowing Zhu Mao's two forces to survive in southern and western Fujian. However, after Peng withdrew from Guidong, he fled back to Nie Du Yingqian on the border of Chongyi, Shangyou, and Suichuan, intending to cut off the connection between Fan's brigade of the Guangdong Army and the large Ganyu Ganzhou. At that time, Fan's brigade had already returned to Yangmei Division on the border of Chongyi Shangyou and the intersection of Nankang and Dayu, and communicated with Li Zhenqiu of Ganzhou and Ye Zhao Zhang Meixin's troops in Dayu Xinfeng. The troops of Li Ming Liu Shaoxian and others of the Eighteenth Army of Suichuan have already been connected with the two divisions of Wang Dongyuan and Chen Guangzhong of Guidong. The bandit, failing to succeed, changed his strategy. At dawn on the 29th of last month, he fiercely attacked Jilong on the border of Jiangxi and Hunan, intending to invade Hunan. At that time, Yu Hanmou, Chen Cheng, Liu Jianxu, etc., ordered Li Ming Liu Shaoxian, Fan Dexing, Wang Dongyuan, and Chen Guangzhong to jointly encircle and suppress the bandits. The two sides fought fiercely. Yesterday, the General Headquarters issued a telegram of victory, which stated that "Peng's bandits attacked Jilong, intending to invade the territory of Hunan. The national army in the area bravely fought back, charging dozens of times and fighting fiercely for a day and a night. Finally, the bandits were defeated on the evening of the 30th. In this battle, more than 2,000 bandits were killed and more than 1,000 guns were seized." As for the southern Jiangxi area, Yu Hanmou, the commander of the First Army of the Guangdong Army, is still in Dayu. The three divisions of Li Zhang and Ye are stationed in Ganyu Dayu Nankang Xinfeng and San'nan to search for scattered bandits and implement rural cleansing. Recently, we received a letter from Ganzhou stating that the peasant bandits in Maodian Jiangkou and other places on the east bank of the Gan River have been cleared by a division of the Guangdong Army.

Another report: After the failure of Zhu Mao Peng Li's various forces to attack Ganzhou a few days ago, Peng Dehuai's remnants temporarily fled to the area of Nankang and Shangyou Yingqian from Tiancun in the Eighth District. The Guangdong First Army then encircled and attacked the bandits. Unable to support themselves, the bandits fled to Rucheng County, Hunan. It is now heard that the bandits in the Rucheng area burned, killed, looted, and plundered. Wang Dongyuan Liu Jianxu of the Hunan Army and Chen Zhang Chen Hanguang, etc., stationed in northern Guangdong, led their troops to encircle the bandits a few days ago. The battle in Rucheng was the fiercest. It is estimated that more than 1,000 bandits were killed, more than 1,000 bandits were wounded, and many bandit guns were seized. Currently, the remaining remnants of the bandits number only 4,000 to 5,000 people with more than 3,000 guns. They have fled to the Shangyou area, and the wounded bandits are being transported to Wenying Yingqian. The 14th Division, 52nd Division of the 18th Hunan Army, and the 2nd and 4th Divisions and the 1st and 2nd Regiments of the 1st Guangdong Army have been mutually contacted and will launch a large-scale encirclement of the bandits, aiming to annihilate them.

Large-Scale Suppression of Banditry in Northern Shandong Province 103

Dispatching Sun and Li as Chief and Deputy Commanders

Zhang Heilian's Troops Successfully Reorganized

Jinan Correspondence: In order to pacify the region, Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, has specially dispatched Sun Tongxuan, commander of the 20th Division, and Li Shuchun, director of the Department of Civil Affairs, as the chief and deputy commanders of the temporary bandit suppression campaign in northern Shandong. They will lead troops to eliminate the accumulated bandits, in order to pacify the region. Furthermore, this morning (the 2nd), a bandit suppression meeting was held in the Provincial Government to discuss the bandit suppression plan. Prior to this, telegrams were sent to the military units stationed in northern Shandong and officials of the local militias, requiring them to send representatives to participate. Therefore, those attending the meeting, in addition to Han Fuqu, Sun Tongxuan, and Li Shuchun, also included Hou Zhaolin, the representative of Li Hanzhang, brigade commander of the 85th Brigade of the 29th Division stationed in Dezhou; He Mengjiu, chief of staff and representative of Liu Guitang, deputy commander of the Shandong Garrison Force stationed in Gaotang; the battalion commander of the mixed battalion representing Zhao Renquan, commander of the Northern Shandong Militia stationed in Linqing; and Liu Shuxiang, chief of staff of the Third Route Army Headquarters. Han first instructed Li Shuchun, Sun Tongxuan, and the various representatives, and then discussed the bandit suppression plan. It is rumored that it has been decided to order Zhang Shulin's unit of the 58th Brigade of the 20th Division to participate in the bandit suppression in northern Shandong. In addition, a portion of mortars and machine guns will be dispatched separately, ordering the 1st Regiment and the brigade headquarters of Zhang's brigade to depart tonight. Sun Tongxuan and Li Shuchun are scheduled to leave Jinan for the north tomorrow (the 3rd) at 4:00 PM, accompanied by the pistol battalion of the 20th Division. It is planned to go to Pingyuan first, and then to the Xiajin area. It is said that the bandits near Pingyuan number only one or two hundred, and the troops should be able to resolve the situation upon arrival.

Regarding Zhang Heilian's troops in southern Shandong, Han Fuqu had previously planned to reorganize them. Xia Ziming was sent to make contact, and there was already some progress. Subsequently, the bandits had a misunderstanding with the local militia and were surrounded and severely attacked by the militia, scattering to Yaozhuang near Baodu Mountain. The situation was extremely dire, and they were almost out of food, resorting to cutting and burning green wheat for sustenance. Recently, Han again sent Xia and Meng Guangshan, director of the headquarters' adjutant office, to make contact. They arrived at Yaozhuang on May 31st and met with Zhang Heilian and Wang Changyou on the morning of June 1st. Zhang made every effort to express his eagerness to surrender, and Li Douyin's unit, entrenched in Lanling Town, more than 150 li from Baodu Mountain, also expressed its willingness to follow Zhang in returning to righteousness and willingly serve Han. Xia and Meng, believing that the negotiations were successful, immediately departed from Yaozhuang for Zaozhuang, and took the Jinpu Railway's second-class train to return to Jinan this morning (the 2nd) to report the results to Han. Han immediately agreed to the reorganization and ordered the troops in southern Shandong to cease their offensive immediately. It is planned to have Liu's troops concentrate in Nan Shahe, and vehicles will be dispatched the day after tomorrow (the 4th) to transport them to Yucheng for reorganization. Meng Guangshan then took the Jinpu Railway train back to Yaozhuang at 9:00 PM tonight (the 2nd) to notify Zhang Heilian and others to assemble and first bring them out of Baodu Mountain in order to await the train at Nan Shahe. Xia Ziming is scheduled to go to Yaozhuang again tomorrow (the 3rd) to assist Meng Guangshan in coordinating everything. (2nd)

Important News Two

Tianjin Circles Express Sympathy for the Movement to Abolish Civil War 105

The Eight-Route Trade Union Advocates Disrupting Civil War Equipment

Sun Chuanfang Discusses the Reasons for Eliminating Civil War

Tianjin Correspondence: The Shanghai circles launched the Great Alliance to Abolish Civil War, and after the telegram arrived in Tianjin, leaders from all circles expressed their approval. The Money Trade Association, the Banking Association, and the City Chamber of Commerce have already issued telegrams expressing their support. Zhang Boling, president of Nankai University, also recently expressed his personal views, stating that the Chinese people have already suffered the pain of civil war. At this critical time of national crisis, when we should be united against foreign aggression, the movement to abolish civil war is a necessary plan. Some people suspect that its future effectiveness will be limited, but he believes that it depends on whether the people truly love their country and are truly awakened. If they truly love their country and are truly awakened, then the entire nation will be determined to join unanimously, and the effectiveness will naturally be great. Zhang also gave a public speech, stating that "For the past twenty years, there has been no solution to the political problems, education has stagnated, and industry and commerce have declined. Today's foreign aggression is caused by internal strife. Why do the Chinese people just sit idly by? I think this is because the people themselves believe that they have no ability, and even if they appeal, it will be ineffective. But now we have reached a critical juncture for the survival of the nation. If we can eliminate internal strife, we will live; if we cannot eliminate internal strife, we will die. Since we clearly recognize that China cannot tolerate any more civil wars and political disputes, the Chinese people should unite and launch a great movement to abolish civil war. If everyone joins, our strength will naturally be great, and even a few ambitious people will probably not dare to advocate for chaos again. Now, all circles in Shanghai have launched a movement to abolish civil war. This is a necessary way to save the fate of the nation and a movement that everyone should participate in. Tianjin is a major commercial port in North China, and its patriotic movement has always been second to none. I hope everyone will unite and express true public opinion, eliminate internal strife, and maintain peace." According to Chen Wenbin, a standing committee member of the City Federation of Trade Unions, each trade union has sent representatives to the meeting, expressing their extreme willingness to join the movement to abolish civil war. However, this movement cannot be achieved by just sending telegrams and issuing declarations. Everyone must unite to be effective. The association will convene a representative assembly of all trade unions in the coming days to discuss concrete measures, with each trade union leading the city's 100,000 workers to sign their names and jointly launch a movement to abolish civil war, using the solid strength of the whole to work effectively. According to the person in charge of the Preparatory Office of the Eight National Railway Trade Unions Federation, the Eight-Route Trade Union Federation is still in the preparatory stage and should be established this month. The association extremely approves of the movement to abolish civil war. In addition to sending separate letters to the eight trade unions under its jurisdiction in the coming days (Jinpu, Beining, Pinghan, Pingsui, Jiaoji, Longhai, Zhengtai, and Daoqing), it will also send separate letters to the trade unions of the Jinghu, Huhang, Yuehan, Guangjiu, Chaoshan, Wuchang, and Zhuping railways, requesting them to lead the workers in launching a movement to abolish civil war. The most effective way in the future is for the trade unions of each railway across the country not to transport troops and military supplies participating in the civil war and to find ways to disrupt its civil war equipment. This idea has been telegraphed to the southbound representatives to contact all circles in Shanghai and to exchange views with the Jinghu and Huhang trade unions in the vicinity. Sun Chuanfang, residing at No. 32 Avenue Dubail in the French Concession, recently told reporters that the changes in national affairs over the past three years have been infinitely regrettable. Now, the movement to abolish civil war, I dare say, is supported by the people of the whole country. It can be said that people share the same heart and the same reason. There have been many civil wars in the past twenty years. If we can eliminate civil war, so that the people who are in dire straits can breathe a sigh of relief, it will be a great thing. I hope this matter is not just empty talk, but emphasizes implementation. Being able to alleviate the suffering of the people by even a little bit is to increase the vitality of the country by a little bit. I also have some opinions on this anti-war movement. Because every civil war must have a cause, I hope everyone can have further measures to completely eliminate the causes of civil war, then civil war can naturally not occur. This is one. Is the war against the Communists within the country a civil war? Some people say that the Communists are an internal problem and cannot be considered a civil war. This is indeed true, but the Communists will definitely defend themselves, saying that they are a revolution, different from bandits who rob homes. The government regards them as bandits. We will also regard them as bandits. However, the government has been suppressing the Reds for several years without seeing them eliminated, and their potential strength is growing day by day. The facts are there and should not be concealed. There must be a major reason for this. In the civil war of the 13th year of the Republic, I once saw it as a confused fight. In fact, except for the Northern Expedition of the Revolutionary Army, almost all the past civil wars can be viewed in this way. The politics of the Qing Dynasty were bad, so there was a revolution. How is the politics of the Republic compared to the Qing government? Children and wealth, good officials act for themselves. If the superiors are good, the inferiors are even worse, while industry and commerce are in difficulty, and the people's livelihood is declining and is ignored. Young people have no way out, and are forced to go to extremes. The government suppresses the Communists every day, but in fact creates Communists every day. Now we do not hope that the government will find a way out for young people, but we hope that it will not close their ears and eyes, so that they have no way to go, but open a line of life for them, so that young people feel that there is light and hope in the future, then it will bring great happiness. This is the second. Japan has seized the three northeastern provinces, as if entering no man's land. We have soldiers who do not defend against foreign aggression, and officials who do not defend the territory. This is truly a global and timeless wonder, and the Chinese people dare not say half a word of disagreement. The 19th Route Army defended against foreign aggression in Shanghai, although it washed away the shame of non-resistance and aroused the national spirit, the result was that the essence of Shanghai was exhausted." As Sun spoke, he sighed repeatedly. This also shows his sympathy for the feelings of abolishing civil war.

Local Correspondence

Taicang 106

A Rice Riot in Xintang City: Xintang City, District 9 of this county, was occupied by the Japanese army for more than a month, and the people suffered heavy losses. On the 27th of last month, the China International Famine Relief Commission sent personnel to the countryside to distribute relief. They first contacted Zhou Tingzhen, the district head, at the district office. The matter was heard by the people, and the heads and deputy heads of six villages, including Liuyao Village, Louxia Village, and Zhujiangqiao Village, and more than a dozen people from the public, were publicly elected to request universal distribution, but to no avail. In the afternoon, hundreds of villagers from more than a dozen villages, together with the village heads and deputy heads, went to the district office again to petition, but still to no avail. Then, an unruly act occurred, resulting in the loss of seventy-two bags of relief rice. The county government believed that District Head Zhou Tingzhen's management was improper, causing the riot, and immediately dismissed him. The vacancy was temporarily filled by Xu Jingwei, an assistant at the district office.

Wuxi 107

A Fierce Battle between Police and Bandits in Xiangzhuang Town: Xiangzhuang Town, near Ganlu in District 11 of the county, is located at the intersection of Changzhou and Wuxi, about two li apart. On the first of this month, as dawn approached, a farmer named Zhou Qingsheng opened the door and went out to lead his ox. In the dim light of dawn, he saw five armed men, whose behavior was suspicious. He immediately questioned them. The soldiers suddenly opened fire, hitting Zhou Qingsheng in the back, the bullet exiting from his chest, and he fainted on the spot. At that time, the 7th Sub-bureau of the Ganlu Public Security Bureau heard the sound of gunfire and immediately dispatched inspectors led by Gu Yi, along with police officers, to pursue and capture them. Subsequently, because it was inconvenient to cross the boundary, they defended in the Wuxi area. However, at this time, the bandits had already lurked in the nearby wheat fields. Upon seeing the police officers, they opened fire and bombarded them. After the police officers bravely resisted, the area was surrounded by water on three sides, and the bandits were trapped. Then, they used a large grave as cover, and the two sides confronted each other for about an hour. Liu, the squad leader of the water police stationed in Ganlu, and Huang Liuchi, the platoon leader of the 3rd Company, 1st Battalion, 259th Brigade of the 87th Division stationed in Changshu, successively led the military police to come to help capture them and to inquire whether any deserters had passed by. Tu Nanxun, the platoon leader of the machine gun company of the regiment, also led his team from Xiangzhuang, At the same time, Ji Abing, a villager, sent two sets of military uniforms with symbols on them, belonging to soldiers of the 3rd Company, 1st Battalion, 518th Regiment of the 87th Division of the Army, saying that they were found next to a coffin. In total, from 6:00 AM to 4:00 PM, the two sides opened fire, resulting in the death of five bandits, who were said to be deserters. In addition, three police officers, Pu Jinsheng, Qian Gengsheng, and He Xingsheng, were shot and killed by the bandits. Four villagers were also wounded by gunfire. Two soldiers of the machine gun company were also killed. All of this has been reported to the County Public Security Bureau and forwarded to the County Court for inspection. As for the wounded villagers, one named Shuang Nuannuan died from his injuries. Pan Gengquan was also seriously injured and is currently being treated at Puren Hospital. The other two, Zhou Wenbing and Zhou Qingsheng, father and son, are both being treated at the Brothers Hospital.

Changzhou 108

Huang Songxiang Shot to Death: Huang Songxiang, a villager in Bianshu Village, District 4 of Wujin County, suddenly heard urgent barking at 1:00 AM on the 30th. He went out to investigate and saw five people holding nets and stealing fish by the ditch. He immediately stepped forward to stop them and was beaten and shot. He fell into the field. Afterward, his family rescued him and took him home, where he died at dawn. One of the perpetrators was Jiang Afu, whom Huang Songxiang recognized when he was dying. Subsequently, the Baoan Corps went to Jiang's house to arrest him. The victim filed a report with the County Court and the County Government on the 3rd. The perpetrator was sent to the county for interrogation today (the 4th).

Notorious Bandit Jiang Xingsheng Arrested: Jiang Xingsheng, a notorious bandit in the northern villages of Wujin County, has committed numerous crimes. He has now been arrested by the police of the 5th Sub-bureau of the Zhenglu Bridge Public Security Bureau. According to his confession, he has committed many crimes. All cases of kidnapping and robbery in the northern villages have been joined by him. On the 3rd, Director Tang Renjie sent police officers to send him to the county for interrogation.

Jiangyin 109

Military Commission Orders Investigation into Intimidation Case: Cai Zhongwei, captain of the 4th Team of the Engineering Training Department of the Military and Political Department, was ordered to come to Cheng during the Shanghai war to rush the construction of rear defense works in the southeastern villages. Because he slapped District Head Shen Tao three times in Houcheng and demanded 200 yuan for rewards, the matter was reported by Ma Zao, director of the office of the Baoan Committee, to the Military Commission, which sent personnel to Cheng to investigate the truth. After returning to Beijing to report, the Military Commission is now consulting the Provincial Government, ordering the Jiangyin County Government to investigate and respond. After receiving the order, Magistrate Ma has ordered the Public Security Bureau to send a sub-bureau chief to investigate and respond.

Rugao 110

Twists and Turns at the County Representative Assembly: At the 5th Rugao County Representative Assembly, after a dispute arose over the election of the presidium, Liu Xikun and 13 others automatically withdrew from the meeting, believing that the meeting was illegal. Sending Personnel to Recover Misappropriated Relief Funds: Zhang Tang, the acting district head of Fengli District, misappropriated 1,000 yuan in relief funds. If Zhang does not return the relief funds in full, he will be sent to the county for interrogation.

Qingjiang 111

A Large Group of Villagers and Christians Kidnapped: On the afternoon of the 29th of this month, more than 90 bandits sneaked to the junction of the 3rd and 4th districts of Huaiyin, each holding a long or short gun, claiming to be soldiers and came to take the case. First, they searched Zhao's Village in Langshi Town for three hours, and then went to the north embankment outside Yuanji to kidnap more than 30 people who were harvesting wheat and picking up wheat in the fields, and shot and killed Yuan Tianfu's son and wounded Liu Fengming and two others, and then roared away. On the same morning, Sun Tingyang, a preacher from Xiaoliu Village in Siyang, was preaching in the market. Just as the Christians were holding a service, a large group of bandits suddenly came and kidnapped Sun and more than 30 other Christians. The Qingjiang Church received the news and yesterday, American pastor Dai Deming took a car to Siyang County to rescue them.

Hangzhou 112

Bandit Leader Zhang Yinbin Arrested: Room 81 of the Huanhu Hotel in Hangzhou City was occupied by a traveler named Zhang Zhen, a young man in Western clothes, who behaved lavishly. Yesterday (the 3rd) at about 10:00 PM, the police station of the 2nd District sent police officers to inspect the hotel and saw that Zhang looked flustered. A letter of introduction to Shanghai for a wooden-cased gun was found on his body. Zhang was taken to the station for questioning. His words were vague. The Provincial Public Security Bureau subsequently received a secret report that Zhang's real name was Zhang Yinbin, a notorious bandit leader in Taihu Lake, and the Baoan Department had offered a reward of 300 yuan for his arrest. He was interrogated strictly and admitted that he was indeed Zhang Yinbin and had had contacts with the bandit leader Zheng Gangda, who had previously been shot. In addition to notifying the Wuxing Public Security Bureau by telegram to investigate the crimes committed by the bandit, he has been prepared to be sent to the Martial Law Command for interrogation.

Luo Tingguang, Zhang Qiyun (university), Sun Yuting (middle school), and Wang Zhixiang (elementary school) have been invited to give speeches on the due date.

Ministry of Education Stipulates Methods for Universities to Recruit Students Returning from Japan to Take Exams and Transfer 114

The Ministry of Education stipulated the methods for universities, colleges, and specialized schools to recruit students returning from Japan to take exams and the treatment after transferring, and issued a notice to national, provincial, and private universities, stating, "After the Northeast Incident, Chinese students in Japan have returned to the country one after another. This Ministry has successively transferred them to various schools for auditing and stipulated temporary relief measures. Now that the Sino-Japanese dispute has not ended, many auditing students are unwilling to return to their original schools and plan to transfer to corresponding schools in the country. The following methods are hereby stipulated for their treatment during entrance exams and after transferring: (1) The schools entered by students in Japan shall be based on the attached list of major specialized schools and above in Japan as the standard for recognizing their qualifications. (2) Graduates of various ordinary higher schools in Japan are allowed to take the entrance exam for the first year of university undergraduate courses. (3) Students of various higher specialized schools and universities in Japan are allowed to apply for the exam based on their grade in their original school. After passing the transfer exam, they can become regular students. A. Those who have not completed the first academic year are allowed to take the exam for the first year. B. Those who have not completed the second academic year are allowed to take the exam for the second year. C. Those who have not completed the third academic year are allowed to take the exam for the third year. D. Those who have not completed the fourth academic year shall be deemed to have completed the third academic year, but they are not restricted by Article 14 of the University Regulations and may be allowed to take the exam for the fourth year. (4) After students returning from Japan pass the transfer exam, the school should calculate the grades of each semester that have been completed in the original school in Japan according to the prescribed standard credits. As for the credits that have been transferred to the school for auditing and have passed the exam, they can be fully recognized. The above methods should be followed by each school and announced to the students. In addition to distributing them separately, the university is hereby ordered to comply. This order includes a list of major specialized schools and above in Japan."

This City

Recent Educational Situation in Shanghai 115

City Schools in War Zones and Near War Zones Will Soon Be Restored

City Schools in Safe Zones and Rural Areas Have Not Been Greatly Affected

The consolidation and restoration of educational undertakings after the completion of the Shanghai war zone is extremely important. The Education News reporter visited the City Education Bureau yesterday to inquire about everything. The following is a summary: When the January 28th Incident occurred and the war was fierce, where the artillery fire reached, the villages and alleys were turned into ruins. The areas of Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong were all turned into scorched earth. All industries were suspended, and the citizens fled. The city's revenue decreased sharply, and municipal construction was almost completely suspended invisibly. The City Education Bureau, in a helpless situation, tried to take care of both sides and distinguished between the safety of the regions, deliberated on the city's revenue, and formulated measures to extend the opening of primary and secondary schools in mid-February. Except for the municipal schools in the war zone and close to the war zone, which could not open, all other primary schools in the safe area and the rural areas behind the war zone were ordered to open as usual. However, primary schools with more grades and higher expenses were subject to separate maintenance measures. Secondary schools jointly found ways to maintain the opening. However, at that time, many citizens moved, and there were fewer students than usual. By the time the war shifted westward in mid-March, the Japanese army had occupied and not withdrawn from the three districts of Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong, and the people had not moved back. Most of the buildings had been reduced to ashes. After the City Education Bureau presented it to the municipal government for approval, it had to temporarily suspend the operation of the municipal primary schools in the three districts and appointed custodians to manage the remaining school equipment in order to allocate and apply it to the overall planning and preparation for the restoration plan in the future. Since the signing of the ceasefire agreement, this entire restoration plan is still awaiting the deliberation and decision of the Shanghai War Zone Post-War Reconstruction Committee. Regarding the temporary consolidation plan, the City Education Bureau believes that the three districts have now been taken over, and the citizens are also moving back to their hometowns one after another. Primary school education cannot be delayed. Therefore, it has sent personnel to the war zone for on-the-spot investigation in the past few days to investigate the damage to the original school buildings of the various primary schools, the extent of the loss of school equipment, and the number of school-age children in the vicinity who are in urgent need of enrollment after the return of residents. It has been decided to formulate a temporary consolidation plan to repair and supplement the original school buildings in the three areas of Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong in the shortest possible time, or to select suitable houses to establish temporary primary schools if the school buildings have been destroyed, in order to maintain the children's schooling. This plan will be implemented as soon as it is approved by the municipal government.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Library Revises Reading Methods 116

No Introduction or Certificate Required, Only One Copper Coin Charged

After the City Chamber of Commerce Library reopened as usual on April 1st, Director Sun Xinpan has been actively carrying out library affairs. In order to popularize reading, no introduction or reading certificate is required to enter the library for reading. Visitors only need to pay one copper coin to read any magazines and books on display. To borrow books outside the library, a deposit of two yuan and a handling fee of one yuan per year are required. After traffic in this city was restored last month, the Ministry's book delivery also resumed, with a delivery fee of only one yuan every six months. If one or two books are borrowed each week, the annual statistics can get a benefit of 100 yuan, so people from all walks of life are very active in visiting the library to read and borrow books. In April, a total of 3,849 books were borrowed, and in May, 7,551 books were borrowed, an increase of more than double. Therefore, it is also making unremitting efforts to solicit donations, deposits, and purchases. Since February, a total of more than 1,100 books and more than 1,200 magazines have been added. The librarians are working hard on registration, cataloging, and delivery work. It is learned that the library also needs to compile an index of commercial materials in various magazines for reference by all circles.

Records of Knocking on the Bell at the Old Temple (13) Zhai Fu Who Does Not Remove the Garden Grass 122

Fifteen

We walked to the entrance of the Normal School. Old Madam Song told the gatekeeper, "We are here to ask for a teacher and want to see the Principal." The gatekeeper said, "The Principal has not yet arrived. Please wait here for a while." Listen! One, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight, nine. This thing rings 'dang, dang, dang' by itself. Old Madam Song said, "This is a self-ringing clock!" What a self-ringing clock! I have long admired its name, and I am so happy to meet it today. We waited and waited, and waited again, until we became impatient, and then we walked inside to take a look. There were thirty or so students sitting in a room. Some words were written on the blackboard, and a gentleman in a suit was teaching the students to read them. The words written on the blackboard did not look like Chinese characters, but the sounds could be clearly distinguished. Everyone was chanting in unison with the teacher, "Ai, Bi, Xi, Di: : :" Old Madam Song said, "They are learning foreign languages." We walked to another identical room, and we could only hear everyone shouting, "Wang, Tu, Si Li: : :" How interesting! Unheard of. Old Madam Song said that we don't need this stuff in the countryside. But I dare not be so dogmatic. Old Madam Song seemed not to like foreign languages very much. She spoke softly in my ear: "Ai, Bi, Xi, Di,

Wang, Tu, Si Li,

Chinese people are farting foreign words."

Haha! Chun Sheng asked us why we were laughing. I told him, and he couldn't help but laugh too.

The bell rang ten times, and the Principal arrived, looking very much like a county magistrate. We explained our purpose and asked him to introduce a really good and capable teacher to go to the countryside. He said, "We have three graduates. I will write a letter to call one to meet with you. Please come back at this time tomorrow." Old Madam Liao was very happy to hear that there were three. She wanted to see all three and then choose one from among them. She was used to using this method to choose a son-in-law. But she was rejected by the Principal. The Principal said, "I will choose the best one to talk to you first. If you think he is very good, he can go to the countryside. If you don't think he is good, I will introduce someone else later." Old Madam Song knew that her method of choosing a son-in-law could not be applied here, so she did not insist. We nodded to the Principal and said goodbye.

There was no hope of going to the countryside today. Old Madam Song took us to play at her sister's house. Her nephew, Young Master Wu, insisted on inviting us to a restaurant to eat big dishes. I guessed it was stewed pork with cabbage, but later I learned that it was foreign food. This meal was actually more strenuous than carrying water. I guessed that Young Master Wu was an expert in eating big dishes, so I carefully learned from him. He used a spoon to drink soup, and I also used a spoon to drink soup. He used a knife to cut meat and a fork to eat it, and I also used a knife to cut meat and a fork to eat it. He didn't move his hands, and I didn't dare to move my hands either. Strange! He drank soup as quietly as a monk eating porridge. So I didn't dare to make any noise when drinking soup either. But Brother Chun Sheng was different. He didn't pay attention to learning from Young Master Wu. He drank soup almost as loudly as an old cow drinking water. He also made a big joke that made everyone's stomachs hurt from laughing. He used a knife to put meat into his mouth to eat. Carelessly, he stabbed his tongue with the knife. I only heard him cry "Ouch!" and he spit out all the food in his mouth. Blood was still dripping and dripping non-stop. It was truly:

"Country bumpkin,

eating big dishes.

Using the knife as chopsticks.

Oh my God!

A piece of the tongue is gone."

Free Talk

Records of Ma Xiangbo, a 93-Year-Old

Japan's "Three Nones" 123

When I was in Japan as a Counselor at the Embassy, it was during the tenure of Minister Li Chunzhai (i.e., Shuchang).

Before becoming a Minister, Li Chunzhai submitted a ten-thousand-word memorial to the Military Affairs Yamen, and the Military Affairs Yamen issued it to Zeng Guofan for use in the camp. Who knew that when Li Chunzhai saw Zeng Guofan, Zeng Guofan told him to "read the Records of the Grand Historian." So Li Chunzhai read the Records of the Grand Historian in the camp, and he read it for more than ten years. This can also be considered a joke.

When I was in Japan, not only did Westerners look down on Japan, but we Chinese also looked down on Japan. At that time, foreigners criticized Japan for having "three nones," which were:

Men have no integrity,

Women have no sense of shame,

Flowers have no fragrance.

Not only did we look down on Japanese men and women, but we also looked down on Japanese flowers and plants. At that time, I was a dignified Counselor at the Chinese Embassy in Japan, and the famous Ito was just a chief in the Ministry. I didn't even know the name of Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi, who was recently assassinated!

Hunger Follows War 124

— Qian Taisheng

War, we acknowledge it as a terrifying demon. Wherever it goes, there is death and bloodshed. Wherever it points, there is plague, homelessness, and no harvest. At the same time, that great demon, "hunger," follows closely behind.

This time, the Battle of Shanghai has caused such devastation to the war zone directly affected that we don't know when we can restore it to its former state.

However, according to the report of the Post-War Relief Committee of Jiangsu,

The urgent need now is to provide relief to those war-torn people who are homeless, without clothing, and without food. Just to build thatched houses, restore farmlands, and improve irrigation, at least 300,000 yuan will be needed. And the area it covers is only six counties, namely Dachang, Jiading, Baoshan, Kunshan, Biaopu, and Changshu, which suffered the greatest damage.

In Dachang, 168 people were sacrificed, and 381 houses were destroyed. In Jiading, more than 100 people died, and 643 houses were burned down. As for the rest, at least 100,000 yuan will be needed for the construction of temporary houses, and the cost of purchasing seeds alone will probably be more than 80,000 yuan. Otherwise, if we do not remedy the situation quickly, next year we will face a situation where there is no rice to eat and no seeds to plant. The year of great famine and disaster will be upon us.

The Most Modern Marriage 125

— Yiqiu

Wang Gongxia, the battalion commander of the 2nd Battalion of the Military Police stationed in Wuxi, is an optimistic revolutionary. He has a very fresh mind and is very frank in his words and actions. Because he is good at laughing, his colleagues gave him the nickname "Happy General."

One day, this interesting Happy General sent out a large number of invitations, writing on them that at a certain time on a certain day, please come to a certain restaurant for a dinner party.

His lover, Ms. Hu Kuang, also invited many of her friends and relatives, saying that at a certain time on a certain day, please come to a certain restaurant for a meal.

At the appointed time, their friends and relatives all arrived at the largest dining room of a certain restaurant. This dining room was divided into two rooms by a large screen. On one side of the room, the sign read "Mr. Wang's Banquet," and on the other side, the sign read "Ms. Hu's Banquet." When the banquet was halfway through, a armed comrade suddenly removed the screen, reconnecting the two rooms into one large room. The guests on both sides looked at each other, bewildered. After a moment, this armed comrade suddenly jumped onto the table and announced to the crowd, "Today is the auspicious day for Mr. Wang Gongxia and Ms. Hu Kuang. They have studied love for many years and decided to get married today. Because this is a memorable day for the beginning of a new life, we have specially invited you to come and enjoy yourselves." At this time, the group of friends who had come to the dinner party without knowing why suddenly realized and uttered a sound of "Ah!" in unison. Thus, this most modern and comical comedy was announced to be completed.

Talking About Shad 126

— Zhu Yuan

Reading my friend Zheng Yimei's notes on "Shad of the Fuchun River" occasionally touched my feelings. I also have some stories about shad. I will write them down in a disorganized way to promote this seasonal fish.

Shad is produced in the river. Every year during the plum rain season, silver scales churn at the head of the Yangtze River. Fishermen cast their nets in the river, catch them, and sell them. Because shad is a seasonal fish, it is only produced in April and May. After this time, it disappears without a trace. The nature of the shad is the same as that of marine fish. It dies immediately when it leaves the water and is difficult to store for long. Therefore, the price of fresh shad is twice as high as that of ordinary fish.

In Jiangsu Province, the area that produces shad is only in the Yangtze River in Zhenjiang and Qiyakou, Changshu. Therefore, those who eat fresh shad usually go to the Yangtze River, wait for the shad to come out, and then cook and eat it. In the past, my old friend Xie Yichang once went to the Yushan Monastery in Zhenjiang to taste the flavor of fresh shad, saying that the fresh shad was fat and delicious, and it was a great pleasure to eat it. Now, the season of plum rain is here again, and the old friend has been away for a long time. Looking up at the sky, I wonder if my old friend also has this feeling.

In Wu, it is customary to give food gifts to relatives and friends during festivals to strengthen friendships. However, due to the emphasis on reciprocity, there are many people with extensive social circles and old friends and relatives. It is impossible to give fresh items to everyone. Often, what is received from A is given to B, and B's items are returned to A. Gifts are exchanged back and forth as festival gifts. During the Dragon Boat Festival, silver-scaled shad fish and zongzi are indispensable festival gifts. However, shad is a light fish that cannot be stored for long, and the price is high. How can those who give gifts buy fresh fish for everyone? As a result, stinky and spoiled shad fish are still given back and forth among relatives and friends, becoming a reward for maids. Therefore, there is a saying that "giving rotten shad fish to people" in the past. Now, the standard of living has increased, and this kind of false custom of giving festival gifts has been somewhat reduced compared to the past. It is unlikely that there will be another "giving rotten shad fish to people" event in society.

In my spare time, I often talked about ruining the scenery with Mr. Cheng Xiaoqing and others. "Cooking shad without scales" and "building a building behind a mountain," "washing feet in a clear stream," and "talking about rice and salt with a beautiful woman" are all things that destroy the atmosphere.

Shad is produced in the river. When it enters the sea, it is called shad. Therefore, the shape and taste of shad and shad are similar. However, shad is especially fresh and palatable. Because "shad has many thorns and carp has a sour taste," it is a regret for gourmets. I don't know that shad is delicious because it has many thorns, just like a beautiful woman can only satisfy the eyes. For those who only eat meat, they cannot appreciate its charm.

Talking About Epidemic Prevention After the War 127

— Guhong

As the saying goes, "After a great war, there will be a great epidemic." When armies are at war, there is bloodshed. After decay and evaporation, epidemics will be bred and spread without end. This time, the violent Japanese invaded our city, burned our houses, and massacred our people. The bodies of the victims were not buried properly. The organic matter contained in them produces various cadaveric poisons through the action of bacteria. The toxins are very strong and spread through the air to the human body, causing death.

Recently, the weather has gradually become hot and the air is dry, making the harm even more severe. Therefore, we should work together to prevent it as soon as possible. The most effective way is to purchase disinfectant and spray it everywhere in the residence to eliminate the germs and prevent the epidemic. The best choice for disinfectant is Yalin Disinfectant produced by Wuzhou Pharmacy. Yalin disinfectant is made of pure ingredients and manufactured with care, with strong bactericidal power. Moreover, it is entirely made in China.

Tidbits 129

— Ping

The Chinese people doubt the meaning of "long-term resistance" and think that these four words are deceptive! In fact, "long-term resistance" does have great effectiveness, but we must distinguish clearly. Some people use it as a verbal advertisement; some people practice it diligently, like the unyielding and courageous Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, which is a true "national salvation army" of long-term resistance, and also a "savior" for recovering lost territory. Our hope is so extravagant, so we must fully meet their material needs, food and military supplies. However, I think there are two things that are disappointing recently: (1) the assistance from all walks of life to the Northeast Volunteer Army is not as enthusiastic as before; (2) the anti-Japanese movement in various places is gradually declining. World News in Brief 130

— Haike

In Salonica, northeastern Greece, there was a lawsuit. An important witness in the case, according to the plaintiff, had already died. The judge ordered him to present a death certificate to prove it. The plaintiff had no choice but to go to the man's grave, dig up the tombstone, and carry it to the court to prove that the man was indeed dead.

In Warsaw, Poland, a young couple came out of the church after getting married. They looked at each other and smiled, and walked slowly shoulder to shoulder. Suddenly, a woman on the side of the road gave them a basket, saying it was a small gift. They accepted it. When they opened it at the wedding banquet, it was a cute baby.

Among the accessories worn by women in British social circles at night, a necklace of fresh flowers has recently become popular. Countless fresh and colorful flowers are woven together. Each necklace costs about five to fifteen shillings, which is ten thousand times more economical than a diamond necklace. However, it must be changed twice every night, because it is difficult to look good when it is wilted.

On the Idea of National Salvation Through Thrift (Part 2) 131

— Narrated by Nie Zeng Jifen, Written by Her Son, Qijie

Later, while at the Liangjiang Governor-General's office, my late father always wanted to maintain a semblance of rural life. He forbade the use of silk for everyday clothing. One day, a guest arrived, and I was wearing a feathered gauze jacket, slightly torn. After the guest left, Duke Wenzheng entered and gazed at it. He asked my mother, "Why is the Manchu girl's clothing so fancy?" My mother quickly replied, "She only wore it for the guest. Feathered gauze is a foreign product, thin and rough in quality, cheaper than serge, and even cheaper than Huzhou crepe. The torn part is Nanjing-woven, only thirty cash per foot. She usually wears this jacket with a cloth vest. When guests arrive, she takes off the vest." My late father set a rule that the expenses for daughters' marriages were limited to 200 gold pieces. The clothing was limited to two boxes, and gold jewelry to two pieces: a flat hairpin and an ear pick. Everything was within these 200 gold pieces. We spun yarn, weaved hemp, sewed, and cooked, with daily assignments. My late father personally inspected our work, leaving us almost no free time. In the past, women's shoes and socks, regardless of wealth, were mostly self-made. We also had to make shoes for our father and brothers as part of our tasks. I continued the spinning work until I was over forty years old, when I lived in the judicial commissioner's office with my late son-in-law. Later, I switched to using a sewing machine. For the past twenty years, this machine has always been placed beside me. Now, at eighty-one, I still enjoy needlework, all thanks to the benefits of the training I received in my youth. The reason I am describing these trivial matters is that the trends of extravagance or thrift in society are initiated by a small number of people. The wives and daughters of nobles are the worst instigators of luxury, often causing trouble for their husbands' conduct and careers. Therefore, my late father was so strict with us. Having received such education early on, I have made it a lifelong habit. I often choose outdated fabrics because they are cheaper. I remember in the year of Jiawu (1894), while at the Shanghai Daotai's office, my late sister-in-law, the wife of Zeng Huimin, came to the office. Seeing the lace I had bought, which had an old-fashioned design, she said, "No one uses this anymore. The current popular foreign lace has fresh and beautiful colors, ten times better than this." I replied, "I have seen it and even bought it for others. However, the price is several times higher than this. Although what I bought is outdated, I like it, and I am happy that the money stays in China and does not flow abroad." My sister-in-law laughed and said, "How much can you save by yourself?" I said, "Even so, if everyone could think this way, or if the Empress Dowager could see this and not love foreign goods and trinkets, then much would be saved."

Record of Dual Buildings in Military Life (69) 132

— Owner of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter 9: Special Train Escapes Guests with False Alarm; Sitting in the Cold Office Turns into Distant Thoughts

It is said that An Yutian, in the compartment, nearly fell when he stepped down to take the seat Ye Zuozhang had offered him, missing the floor. In that critical moment of shock, fortunately, Mao Deshun quickly reached out from behind and helped him, preventing him from making a fool of himself in public. However, a teacup on the shelf in front of him had been knocked over, and tea was dripping. His actions were frivolous and lacked decorum. After sitting down, he couldn't help but blush, feel his heart pound, and deeply regret his recklessness. Ye Zuozhang, on the other hand, was magnanimous and didn't mind at all. He allowed the attendants to wipe up the tea stains and still asked An Yutian questions with a smiling face. At first, he only asked about common things like his place of origin and education, which An Yutian could easily answer. This allowed him to slowly calm down and secretly observe Ye Zuozhang's demeanor. Although he was short in stature, his spirit was very vibrant. His eyes were bright and piercing, seeming to possess immense authority. His speech was loud and clear, his words humorous and quirky, both rough and charming. When he mentioned Liang Xiaoyun, he even patted An Yutian on the shoulder and said, "You are more fortunate to marry such a good wife than I am to be a military governor! Why did you still come to me? But since Xiaoyun Lao Ba recommended you, someone he appreciates must certainly be without fault. How could I not rely on you?" Having said that, he shook his monkey-like head and laughed heartily. The laughter made An Yutian's hair stand on end. He suddenly thought, "Isn't he clearly laughing at me as a 'soft rice king' who relies entirely on connections through women to seek official position? So he dares to treat me as a source of amusement and openly insult me. According to the principle that a scholar can be killed but not humiliated, I must show him some integrity!" Immediately, this feeling of anger dispelled the shyness and embarrassment he had felt earlier. He straightened his back with righteous indignation and said, "That is a personal love affair and not worth mentioning. I came to see the military governor because I have long heard that the governor is enthusiastic about bringing benefits to the region and needs talented people to help. Therefore, I introduced myself to the governor and proposed an idea for clearing out bandits and pacifying the people. I am willing to have my humble opinion adopted and put into action, so that I can say what I can do and do what I say. I can quickly organize those bandits and militias that have been in contact for a long time into elite troops to serve the country. Once the banditry in the region is cleared, the governor can expand his strength. I will repay the governor and my fellow villagers, fulfilling my lifelong ambition. That is the greatest happiness!" Although this speech was delivered with great vigor, its meaning was still disjointed and not necessarily impressive.

The Silk and Tea Industry: The Jiangning Cocoon Market Effectively Ceased Operations 142

Cocoon Merchants Few, Cocoon Prices Low

Farmers Drying Cocoons Themselves

In Jiangning and surrounding rural areas, the number of silkworm farmers this year is only 20-30% of last year's. However, in the villages near the city, improved breeds distributed by silkworm breeding societies are being cultivated, and graduates from silkworm schools are providing guidance. Therefore, although the weather has been unfavorable, the damage has not been significant, and the cocoon yield is still good. However, the cocoon exchanges have not been leased out, and only one or two merchants are buying at suppressed prices. The farmers' costs are not low, and they are generally unwilling to sell cheaply. The highest cocoon price is only a little over 20 yuan, and the lowest is only 14 or 15 yuan. Farmers are mostly taking them back to dry themselves using traditional methods, or pooling funds to entrust cocoon merchants to dry them on their behalf, in order to spin their own native silk. Thus, it is said that the cocoon market has effectively ceased operations.

Yesterday, the demand for imported rice from both local and out-of-town buyers was weak. For the past few days, merchants from inland areas have been waiting and watching. Only this street continued to offer it in minimal amounts. The market situation continued to soften, and the price decreased slightly by six or seven fen. However, due to the market price decline, Hubei merchants gradually saw a suitable point and attempted a small transaction of 300 bags. This slightly stabilized the market. The overall market opened with 500 bags of Xiaojiao rice, priced at 10 yuan, 8 jiao and a half to 7 jiao; 1,000 bags of Min Dang rice, priced at 11 yuan to 10 yuan and 9 jiao; and 200 bags of Saigon No. 1, priced at 11 yuan and 9 jiao and a half. Except for the bags bought by Hubei merchants, all were taken by local rural households.

It is expected that foreign firms will continue to peddle imported rice, but without any takers, there will be no transactions, and prices will continue to decline. A new ship with a scheduled delivery of Xiaojiao rice has arrived and is scheduled to dock and unload today. The number is estimated to be around 40,000 to 50,000 bags.

Futures Market Resumes; First Act - Uniform Price Drop Across All Months 146

Yesterday, the futures flour market officially resumed trading. The trading in both markets was quite lively. Because of the good weather, the price of foreign wheat also decreased by about three jiao. In addition, actual sales were sluggish, and the manufacturers' inventories remained as abundant as before. When trading opened last year, the price for July was 2 taels and 2 fen. Later, manufacturers such as Fuxin and Fufeng sold off their inventory, and confidence waned. For this reason, the prices for August and September gradually trended downward. The opening prices for October and November were flat at first, but then showed improvement as customers bought in small amounts. However, when trading opened in the afternoon, the market sentiment fluctuated greatly. Compared to the morning prices, the price continued to fall by about 2 fen. The reason for the decline is that manufacturers indicated that they would sell as much as possible based on the July standard, intending to clear their inventories to prepare for the smooth entry of new wheat. As a result, people panicked, and the market showed a continuous downward trend. The total price drop between the opening and closing prices for July and August was 3 fen and 2.5 li, for September it was 2 fen and 2.5 li, and for October and November it was 1 fen. The total number of transactions was 364,000 bags.

Textiles: Feathersatin and Woolen Cloth Sell Well In a Timely Manner 147

Prices of New and Old Goods Fluctuate Differently

As the weather has gradually become warmer in recent days, the trade in woolen fabrics has gradually decreased. Only summer and white goods are currently selling well. Yesterday, there was a great need for feathersatin from buyers. The Guild's wholesale was also substantial, purchased by local merchants. Furthermore, newly arrived feathersatin was selling better. Most ordinary brands were priced at more than 3 taels, as their quality was superior and suitable for Western clothing. Old-stock plaid and striped feathersatin were also selling very briskly in the market, and the prices were extremely cheap. Yesterday, Xinyi goods sold for 1 tael and 8 qian, Hengli for 1 tael and 6 qian and a half. Other miscellaneous brands of plaid and striped goods were selling for only 1 tael and 5 or 6 qian per yard.

Metals: British Galvanized Iron - Thick Gauges in Demand; Thin Gauges Lack Sales 148

The market for British galvanized iron had previously been weak due to an oversupply of goods and enthusiastic arrivals, resulting in a decline in standards. For example, No. 24 was estimated at 9 taels and 2.5 qian per dan, No. 26 at 10 taels and 0.25 qian, No. 28 at 11 taels, 9 qian for 3.7 chi and 7 qian and 8 fen for 3.6 chi. However, there were few buyers. In recent days, the business of out-of-town merchants has suddenly flourished, and the buying and selling of local construction merchants has also been very good. As a result, there are not enough goods in the market to meet demand, and market prices have gradually increased. No. 24 can now be estimated at 9 taels and 7.5 qian per dan, No. 26 at 10 taels and 5 qian, and No. 28 at 11 taels and 2.5 qian. No. 24 is the most scarce in the market. Because the supply of thin gauges in the market exceeds demand, and there are fewer purchases from the northern route, standards remain difficult to increase. 3.7 chi is estimated at 9 qian 1 or 2 fen per sheet, and 3.6 chi at around 8 qian. It is said that if business picks up in the coming days, prices may rise further.

Coal: Sales of Processed Coal Greatly Reduced 149

The processed coal business in Shanghai has been greatly affected since the Shanghai War. Most of the glass factories in Zhabei have been destroyed and have stopped production. In addition, as the weather is getting warmer, the use of stoves in Western residences has also gradually decreased, and sales are becoming scarce. Recently, the entire city has only sold more than 30 tons per day. As a result, the wholesale price has fallen by 2 yuan per ton. The current wholesale price for lump coal is 34 yuan per ton, screened lump coal is 32 yuan, mixed coal is 28 yuan, and coal ash is 14 yuan.

Local News

Joint Sino-Japanese Committee Discussed Complete Withdrawal of Japanese Troops Yesterday 150

Result Still No Definite Deadline

Regarding the issue of the complete withdrawal of Japanese troops, our Joint Committee has already sent a letter to the Chairman of the Joint Committee, Mr. Ke Yinhang. We have recently received a reply from the Japanese side, stating that the troops in all areas have been completely withdrawn, leaving only a small number of military police. Our committee members believe that the Japanese reply did not pay attention to our letter. Therefore, they sent another letter to Ke Yinhang the night before last, urging him to expedite the withdrawal of Japanese troops in accordance with the agreement. The main points of the letter were: According to the provision in the May 5th agreement to restore the situation before January 28th, Japanese troops are still stationed east of Songhu Road and in the Sha Jinggang area, which is in complete violation of the agreement. Please maintain the spirit of cooperation since January and uphold the agreement, etc. After receiving the letter, Ke Yinhang has already notified the other committee members.

Bilateral Discussion Yesterday at 10:30 AM, our committee member Yu Hongjun and Japanese committee member Okazaki Katsuo discussed the issue of the complete withdrawal of Japanese troops at the Joint Committee office. Okazaki first stated that the stationing of Japanese troops in District D was temporary. In areas such as Sha Jinggang, the troops are stationed for the purpose of patrolling and protecting Japanese residents due to their panic. Chinese authorities can still carry out all administrative powers in the city. Only a small number of military police are stationed at the Wusong Yarn Factory, Tongwen Academy, and Toyota Yarn Factory. Before the war, marines were also stationed there. Furthermore, the Japanese side has ordered these military police not to leave the factory premises. He requested understanding. Yu then refuted this, saying that he had never heard of Japanese marines being stationed at Tongwen Academy before. The municipal government can be responsible for the protection of Japanese residents without the need for Japanese troops to interfere. He reiterated that the stationing of Japanese troops in various places violated the agreement and hoped that they would withdraw immediately in accordance with the agreement, giving a deadline. Okazaki replied that the issue of a deadline needed to be discussed further before a reply could be given. At a little after 11 AM, the meeting adjourned without a result.

Negotiations on Road Construction Beyond the Border 151

Results of Negotiations Between Municipal Government and Public Works Bureau

A Complete Solution Has Been Drafted

Complete Administrative Sovereignty Rests with Our Country

Regarding the issue of all administrative powers related to the construction of roads beyond the border by the Public Concession, Municipal Government representative Yu Hongjun and Public Works Bureau representative Feixindun have been negotiating for several months. By 10:00 AM yesterday, the opinions of both parties began to converge, and the negotiations came to an end. It is expected to be completely decided after both parties seek instructions from their superiors. The details are as follows:

Yu Hongjun's Speech Yesterday at 10:00 AM, Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun met with Public Works Bureau Secretary-General Feixindun to continue discussions on the issue of road construction beyond the border. They dispersed after about half an hour. According to Yu, the representatives of the Municipal Government and the Public Works Bureau have reached a complete solution to the issue today (i.e., yesterday), and it is expected to be completely decided after both parties seek instructions from their superiors. The content includes police and public works matters, but complete administrative sovereignty rests with us. The detailed articles are temporarily not convenient to be published.

Organization of Special Police The Damei Evening News reported that the Public Concession Public Works Bureau Information Office announced at noon on the 4th that representatives from the Chinese authorities and the Public Works Bureau were negotiating on the issue of road construction beyond the border, hoping to reach an agreement. It has now progressed to the point where concrete proposals can be submitted to the Chinese authorities and the Public Works Bureau for consideration. Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, who is representing the Chinese authorities, has made a similar statement. As for the content of the negotiations, although it has not yet been officially confirmed by the Public Works Bureau, according to the Damei Evening News, the police power and sovereignty of road construction beyond the border are the main issues in this Shanghai negotiation. According to recent proposals, the Chinese government retains sovereignty and complete management rights over road construction beyond the border, but special police may be organized with foreign personnel as supervisors. This supervisor and all employees will be under the command of the Shanghai Municipal Government, and their salaries will also be paid by the Shanghai Municipal Government. However, it must be solemnly stated that what has been agreed upon in Shanghai this time is purely informal and is only the basis for formal negotiations in Nanjing.

Public Works Bureau Information According to a message released by the Public Concession Public Works Bureau Information Office yesterday, representatives from the Public Concession Public Works Bureau and the Chinese authorities are consulting on the basis of an agreement on the issue of roads outside the boundary, and have now reached a considerable degree, with a concrete plan to be submitted to the Public Works Bureau and the Chinese authorities.

History of Road Construction Beyond the Border The start of road construction beyond the boundary by the Public Concession dates back to 1862. At that time, the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom army suddenly disturbed Songhu, and the people fled to the concession. At that time, the concession area was still very small, with the racecourse as the boundary at its westernmost point. As there were many refugees, the Public Concession authorities sought to expand westward, immediately building Jing'an Temple Road, from Nicheng Bridge to Jing'an Temple. In 1866, General Gordon helped the Chinese authorities defeat the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom army, and then used the pretext to build Gordon Road, Xinza Road, etc. By 1899, road construction beyond the boundary had expanded to thirteen miles. Subsequently, the northeast, west, and south sections also actively expanded outward. By 1918, the total area reached 29,893 miles. By 1925, it had increased to 48,093 miles. According to estimates at the time, the Public Works Bureau spent a total of 10,039,110 taels on road construction beyond the boundary. The cost of land purchase during road construction beyond the boundary was 2,894,660 taels. This was the value at the time. However, because of this, the Chinese authorities and the Public Works Bureau have repeatedly engaged in negotiations, the number of which is now unknown. If the municipal authorities can thoroughly resolve this matter, it will reduce many disputes between Chinese and foreign authorities at sea in the future.

Large Artillery Shell Found in Huangpu River 159

The Continental News reported that on Thursday, while working near the Huishan Wharf, a dredger of the Huangpu Bureau found an unexploded large artillery shell, which was 20 feet long and 8 inches in diameter. During the recent Sino-Japanese military conflict, Chinese armored trains fired artillery at the Japanese consulate near the Mcgregor Road Bridge, and many of the shells fell into the Huangpu River. The Huangpu Bureau is now afraid that the dredger will touch the unexploded shells that are submerged in the river and cause an explosion, which will not only damage the dredger but also hinder nearby navigation. Therefore, it is heard that the bureau has temporarily suspended work in that area.

Post-War Relief Committee Inspects Jiading and Liuhe Yesterday 160

Most Refugees in Various War Zones Have Returned

Jiading Suffered 500 Casualties and 10 Million Losses

The Post-War Relief Committee, in accordance with the inspection procedure, conducted its final inspection of the five districts of Jiading, Liuhe, Luodian, Dachang, and Liuhang yesterday. All members gathered at the United Society and departed on time. The details are as follows:

First Inspection of Dachang Yesterday's inspection team remained the same as yesterday. On the receiving committee side, Zha Nanqiang was added to accompany and entertain. They departed in three cars at 9:20 AM and arrived at Dachang Huiji Baohua Temple at 10:00 AM. The temple was not damaged after the war, and all personnel disembarked to conduct a detailed investigation. The cement archway built by Xi Huirun in April of the 19th year of the Republic was blown off in front of the temple. The center of the Zoumatang bank was blown into a hole, which was more than a zhang deep. Further in, the interior of the Weituo Hall and the Daxiong Treasure Hall were not damaged. Only a few flat houses west of the hall were destroyed. About a li west of Baohua Temple is the Dragon King Temple, which was completely destroyed, with nothing left. There were also two refugee trenches dug next to the temple, more than a zhang deep. It is said that during the tense war, Japanese planes frequently bombed, and a group of poor people hid here. Then, they entered Dachang Town and patrolled for a week. There are about 500 shops in the whole town, with the eastern part being the most severely burned. After the First Regiment of the Capital Security Police stationed in the town entered to inquire about everything in detail, the head of the regiment had already gone to the capital. The company commander then led them to visit the team and successively dug out and collected 31 boxes of machine gun bullets, hundreds of hand grenades, 20 aircraft bombs, and electric thunder mines. After reading, they boarded the car and left the town.

Current Situation in Jiading After the inspection of Dachang was completed, they drove directly to Jiading County via Liuhang and Luodian, arriving at 11:30 AM. The county magistrate of the county, Mr. Pan Zhongjia, had heard the news beforehand and, along with the Director of Education Jin Chengyong, the Director of the County Public Security Bureau Shen Jinghua, the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce Chen Peiqing, and the county police brigade, waited outside the east gate of Jiading County. When the inspection team arrived, they raised their banners to welcome them. The members of the committee then got out of the car, changed to 24 rickshaws, and entered the city. After going to the county education bureau for a short rest and lunch, they took rickshaws again, accompanied by the county magistrate and others, to inspect the northeast and east gates, which were the most severely damaged. The scene in the whole town was appalling. According to Pan, the county has a total area of ​​640,000 mu, covering about 1,200 square miles, and is divided into eight districts. The jurisdiction of each district office is (District 1) Chengxiang, (District 2) Nanxiang, (District 3) Xujiahang, (District 4) Waigang, (District 5) Loutang, (District 6) Huangdu, (District 7) Ji Wangmiao, (District 8) Anting. There are more than 67,000 households in the whole city, and the population is more than 290,000 according to the latest survey. During the tense war, everyone fled, leaving only 170 people in the whole city. The Japanese invaders entered the city on March 3 and withdrew on May 8, occupying it for two months and six days. People's belongings were looted. According to the surveys conducted in the past few days, more than 2,600 households had their houses burned, and 375 people died (not including the unnamed). The Anlu Cotton Weaving Factory in the county was completely destroyed, with losses estimated at more than 1 million yuan (i.e., the Anlu factory on Damalu Road). The commercial losses in the county were estimated at more than 8 million yuan, with the greatest losses outside the north gate. The north gate belongs to Huangqingxiang and was burned for a day and night on March 3, and it is not easy to restore it. According to Shen Jinghua, the director of the Public Security Bureau, since taking over on the 8th of last month, the local area has been peaceful. In the past ten days, they have used silver dollars to buy back many leftover shells, including 140,000 bullets, 24 boxes of hand grenades, 15 artillery shells, two aircraft bombs, and 20 machine gun mounts. When resisting the invaders, only four policemen were killed in Xuhang. Most of the fleeing people have returned, and the shops are also trying to open, but the number is very small. Sanitary matters after the war are extremely important, so they are currently engaged in inspecting the drinking water in public and private wells.

Final Inspection of Various Towns The inspection of Jiading took the longest time, and it was not completed until 2:15 PM. The members of the inspection team then boarded the car and turned to Liuhe, arriving at the Xinzha Bridge in the town at 3:00 PM. They parked the car and walked east, passing through Nanxiang Street to the Taicang Second District Office to rest. According to the statistics of the losses in the war by the office, 70 people died, 24 were injured, and more than 50 households had their houses burned, totaling 200 rooms. After the inspection of Liuhe was over, they arrived at Luodian at 4:30 PM. The town belongs to Baoshan County, bordering Jiading to the west, Taicang to the north, Shanghai to the south, and Wusong to the east, with an area of ​​150 square miles and a population of more than 14,000. It governs 29 villages and one town. After the war, more than 50 households had their houses burned, 20 people died, and clothing, food, livestock, and agricultural products were looted, totaling more than 1.1 million yuan. After the inspection there was completed, due to the urgency of time, they were unable to inspect Liuhang according to the planned schedule and returned to Shanghai at 4:20 PM, arriving at the United Society at 5:45 PM.

This Newspaper Plans to Publish the Shen Bao Monthly 162

This newspaper, with the longest history among domestic dailies, is already recognized by the Chinese people. On its 50th anniversary, it published "The Most Recent Fifty Years" as a commemoration. Time flies, and the 60th anniversary is approaching again.
